The service in the lobby is really good. There will be a special person to receive you when you arrive at the store. The front desk staff did not perfunctorily check in because there were many people during the holiday. They also patiently answered the travel guide about the dead efficiency. Seeing that we were with children, the porter took the initiative to take our luggage to the room. The room service is standard. It takes half a day to send something. The stew in the evening is just a few mung beans and water. It is better not to send it. The low score is given to the hot spring center. There is no service. There is only one waiter sitting at the door to give hand cards. The locker room is unmanaged and looks dirty and messy. When taking a hot spring bath, the children want to eat but there is nothing. Even the waiter can't see it. The most important point is that the sanitation of the hot spring pool is too poor. I don't know if it is cleaned every day. Why is there such a big difference in service in the same hotel? The hotel management staff should think about it carefully.

It is small and uncomfortable to sleep on. Moreover, there is a large bed and a small bed. There is only a bedside table on one side of the big bed and a bedside table on the other side of the small bed. There is no bedside table to put things on, and the small bed is like a makeshift bed. Secondly, the shower room and toilet room share the same glass sliding door, and only one of them can be used at the same time. In addition, the partitions between the bathroom and the bedroom are made of frosted glass. Frosted glass with relatively high transparency can be seen by people outside if someone in the bathroom has not yet put on clothes after taking a shower. In addition, there is a common door between this room and the next room. This door cannot be opened, but you can hear what the next door is saying through this door. Finally, when I left, I was told that the price of a large bottle of Nongfu Spring in the room was 22 yuan, but I did not pay attention to the sign saying that I had to pay for it. I was told by the hotel that there was a small piece of paper with 22 yuan on the bottle cap. How big is the bottle cap of Nongfu Spring? , it is difficult for guests to see it. If communication fails, the deposit will be deducted.

msg:It's a bit far from Shanghai to Yunhe Terraced Fields. I want to find a place to rest on the way. This hotel has a very high score on Ctrip, so this is it. After coming here, I was pleasantly surprised. It was really great!
1) Location: It's very close to the "Shenxianju" scenic spot, and there is a local top-ranked restaurant two kilometers around. The taste is great! And the price is very affordable, and the quantity is also very large.
2) Service: Manager Zhao of the hotel room depar**ent and Xiaoying at the front desk welcomed us very warmly. Since I booked a different room type the next day, they helped us to change it early the next morning so that we could rest in time when we came back to the scenic spot. Room; Manager Zhao knew that we had clothes to wash and even brought a drying rack. The room on the second day was also upgraded. They also introduced in detail how to play in the scenic spot to take beautiful photos. The service is really great! Thank you for letting us spend two wonderful nights here!
3) Facilities: The hotel has just opened, the facilities are very new, and the room is very large; the room offers fruits and snacks; sweet soup is provided in the evening; in addition, the hotel's Japanese-style hot spring is great! The water quality is natural, there is a large pond, and there are more than a dozen small ponds, all of which are room-to-room, including beer, jasmine, rose, coffee, honeysuckle and so on. In-house guests have a discount of only 50 yuan per person, which is very worthwhile to experience. After the National Day is the off-season, we have a private venue today, and there are almost no people. The hot spring facilities are also great! Very clean!
4) Breakfast: It is also one of the highlights. There are various local snacks, many varieties, and they are all very delicious! like!
Manager Zhao said that the most beautiful season here is winter, and the scenery of Shenxianju is like a fairyland. At that time, we will come back to see the beautiful scenery and soak in the hot springs. Will highly recommend to my friends!

Booked a business room, 776 one night, two nights, directly asked me to charge 2500, without any explanation or reason, I asked why the charge was 2500, the front desk next to it said 2000 is fine, and the rest is a deposit. It can be seen that the sense of service is weak, and there is no uniform standard for charging.

It can be seen that the hotel is very casual. When there are customers in the hotel, it focuses on its own interests. It will cut off the power and stop the elevator at will, without considering the interests of the customers.
4. When you check out, you missed a charger, which socket was definitely missed, and called the front desk, the front desk said there was no. It is also very lacking in cleaning management.
Highlights:
1. There are hot springs and swimming pools, so you can enter, which is more convenient.
2. The young man in the lobby is very enthusiastic and will help with luggage, open the door, etc.
